          (1): Conv2d(128, 128, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1), bias=False)
          (2): BatchNorm2d(128, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
        )
      )
      (1): MaxPool(
        (op): Sequential(
          (0): MaxPool2d(kernel_size=3, stride=1, padding=1, dilation=1, ceil_mode=True)
          (1): Conv2d(128, 128, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1), bias=False)
          (2): BatchNorm2d(128, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
        )
      )
      (2): ConvBnRelu(
        (op): Sequential(
          (0): Conv2d(128, 128, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1), bias=False)
          (1): BatchNorm2d(128, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
          (2): ReLU(inplace)
        )
      )
      (3): ConvBnRelu(
        (op): Sequential(
          (0): Conv2d(128, 128, kernel_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1, 1), bias=False)
          (1): BatchNorm2d(128, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
          (2): ReLU(inplace)
        )
      )
    )
  )
  (reducefeature1): FeatureReduce(
    (conv): Conv2d(64, 64, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1))
    (bn): BatchNorm2d(64, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
    (up): Upsample(size=(113, 225), mode=bilinear)
  )
  (reducefeature2): FeatureReduce(
    (conv): Conv2d(128, 64, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1))
    (bn): BatchNorm2d(64, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
    (up): Upsample(size=(113, 225), mode=bilinear)
  )
  (featurefusion): Sequential(
    (0): Conv2d(128, 128, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1), bias=False)
    (1): BatchNorm2d(128, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
    (2): ReLU(inplace)
  )
  (laneline): Sequential(
    (0): Conv2d(128, 32, kernel_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1, 1))
    (1): BatchNorm2d(32, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
    (2): ReLU(inplace)
    (3): Conv2d(32, 16, kernel_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1, 1))
    (4): BatchNorm2d(16, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
    (5): ReLU(inplace)
    (6): Conv2d(16, 19, kernel_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1, 1))
    (7): Upsample(size=(449, 897), mode=bilinear)
  )
)
